\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a65a176508b404f80e5f5abd31456712e}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a65a176508b404f80e5f5abd31456712e} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!blend\_poisson\_bf@{blend\_poisson\_bf}}
\index{blend\_poisson\_bf@{blend\_poisson\_bf}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{blend\_poisson\_bf()}{blend\_poisson\_bf()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::blend\+\_\+poisson\+\_\+bf (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{array1,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{array2,  }\item[{const int}]{iterations = {\ttfamily 500},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+mask = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Blends two arrays using Poisson blending with a brute-\/force solver. 

This function performs Poisson blending between {\ttfamily array1} and {\ttfamily array2} over a specified number of iterations. Optionally, a mask can be provided to control the blending regions.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em array1} & The first input array. \\
\hline
{\em array2} & The second input array. \\
\hline
{\em iterations} & The number of iterations for the blending process (default\+: 500). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+mask} & Optional pointer to an array defining the blending mask. If null, blending is applied globally. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The blended array resulting from the Poisson blending operation.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{hydraulic\_schott@{hydraulic\_schott}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hydraulic\_schott()}{hydraulic\_schott()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::hydraulic\+\_\+schott (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{int}]{iterations,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus,  }\item[{float}]{c\+\_\+erosion = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{c\+\_\+thermal = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{c\+\_\+deposition = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{flow\+\_\+acc\+\_\+exponent = {\ttfamily 0.8\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{flow\+\_\+acc\+\_\+exponent\+\_\+depo = {\ttfamily 0.8\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{flow\+\_\+routing\+\_\+exponent = {\ttfamily 1.3\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{thermal\+\_\+weight = {\ttfamily 1.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{deposition\+\_\+weight = {\ttfamily 2.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+flow = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Simulates hydraulic erosion and deposition on a heightmap using the Schott method. 

This function performs hydraulic erosion on the given heightmap {\ttfamily z} over a specified number of iterations. It includes parameters for controlling erosion, deposition, and flow routing. Optional flow accumulation can also be computed and stored in the {\ttfamily p\+\_\+flow} array.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em z} & The heightmap array to be modified. Heights are updated in-\/place. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em iterations} & The number of iterations for the hydraulic erosion process. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em talus} & An array defining the slope threshold for erosion. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em c\+\_\+erosion} & Erosion coefficient (default\+: 1.\+0f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em c\+\_\+thermal} & Thermal erosion coefficient (default\+: 0.\+1f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em c\+\_\+deposition} & Deposition coefficient (default\+: 0.\+2f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em flow\+\_\+acc\+\_\+exponent} & Exponent controlling the influence of flow accumulation on erosion (default\+: 0.\+8f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em flow\+\_\+acc\+\_\+exponent\+\_\+depo} & Exponent controlling the influence of flow accumulation on deposition (default\+: 0.\+8f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em flow\+\_\+routing\+\_\+exponent} & Exponent controlling flow routing behavior (default\+: 1.\+3f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em thermal\+\_\+weight} & Weight of thermal erosion effects (default\+: 1.\+5f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em deposition\+\_\+weight} & Weight of deposition effects (default\+: 2.\+5f). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em p\+\_\+flow} & Optional pointer to an array for storing flow accumulation data. If null, flow data is not returned (default\+: nullptr).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://hal.science/hal-04565030v1/document}{\texttt{ https\+://hal.\+science/hal-\/04565030v1/document}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a87339ed12fc8a86b1f59e351b06e67e6}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a87339ed12fc8a86b1f59e351b06e67e6} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!thermal\_scree@{thermal\_scree}}
\index{thermal\_scree@{thermal\_scree}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{thermal\_scree()}{thermal\_scree()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void hmap\+::gpu\+::thermal\+\_\+scree (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{talus,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{zmax,  }\item[{int}]{iterations = {\ttfamily 10},  }\item[{bool}]{talus\+\_\+constraint = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs thermal scree erosion on a heightmap. 

This function applies a thermal erosion process that redistributes material from steeper slopes to flatter areas, simulating talus formation. The process iterates a given number of times to achieve a more stable terrain profile.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em z} & The heightmap to be modified in-\/place by the erosion process. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em talus} & The threshold slope angles that determine where material is moved. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em zmax} & The maximum allowed elevation for erosion effects. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em iterations} & The number of erosion iterations to apply (default\+: 10). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em talus\+\_\+constraint} & Whether to enforce a constraint on the talus slope (default\+: true). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em p\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+map} & Optional pointer to an array that stores the deposited material per cell. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a112228c7b9ebff5463329da76d00fff1}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a112228c7b9ebff5463329da76d00fff1}

\index{thermal\_scree@{thermal\_scree}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}

\index{basalt\_field@{basalt\_field}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{basalt\_field()}{basalt\_field()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::basalt\+\_\+field (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{warp\+\_\+kw = {\ttfamily 4.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{large\+\_\+scale\+\_\+warp\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{large\+\_\+scale\+\_\+gain = {\ttfamily 6.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{large\+\_\+scale\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 3.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+warp\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+gain = {\ttfamily 7.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.08\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{small\+\_\+scale\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 10.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{small\+\_\+scale\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.1\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{small\+\_\+scale\+\_\+overlay\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.002\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{rugosity\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{rugosity\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{bool}]{flatten\+\_\+activate = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{float}]{flatten\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{flatten\+\_\+amp = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a synthetic procedural terrain resembling basaltic landforms. 

This function creates a multi-\/scale procedural field combining large, medium, and small-\/scale Voronoi-\/based patterns, noise warping, and optional flattening, simulating the morphology of fractured basalt or volcanic terrains. The terrain is constructed using a combination of Voronoi diagrams (via {\ttfamily voronoi\+\_\+fbm}) and fractal noise ({\ttfamily noise\+\_\+fbm}), layered with frequency-\/domain manipulations and amplitude/gain controls at each scale.

The final output is a heightmap represented as an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}}, normalized and composed of\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Large-\/scale cellular patterns with smoothed Voronoi edge distances.
\item Medium and small-\/scale structures introducing finer surface variation.
\item Optional rugosity (fine detail) and flattening to simulate erosion or flow effects.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Output resolution (width x height) of the field. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Base wave numbers (frequency) for the terrain features. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Initial seed used for deterministic random generation. \\
\hline
{\em warp\+\_\+kw} & Frequency of the warping noise that displaces Voronoi positions. \\
\hline
{\em large\+\_\+scale\+\_\+warp\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of displacement for large-\/scale Voronoi warping. \\
\hline
{\em large\+\_\+scale\+\_\+gain} & Gain adjustment applied to the large-\/scale features. \\
\hline
{\em large\+\_\+scale\+\_\+amp} & Final amplitude of the large-\/scale height contribution. \\
\hline
{\em medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio} & Scaling factor for the frequency of the medium-\/scale patterns. \\
\hline
{\em medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+warp\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of warping for the medium-\/scale displacement. \\
\hline
{\em medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+gain} & Gain control for medium-\/scale modulation. \\
\hline
{\em medium\+\_\+scale\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of the medium-\/scale heightmap. \\
\hline
{\em small\+\_\+scale\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio} & Frequency ratio for small-\/scale details. \\
\hline
{\em small\+\_\+scale\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude of small-\/scale pattern contribution. \\
\hline
{\em small\+\_\+scale\+\_\+overlay\+\_\+amp} & Additional overlay strength for repeating the small-\/scale pattern. \\
\hline
{\em rugosity\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio} & Frequency ratio for high-\/frequency noise applied as fine roughness. \\
\hline
{\em rugosity\+\_\+amp} & Strength of the rugosity (high-\/frequency modulation). \\
\hline
{\em flatten\+\_\+activate} & Enables or disables the final flattening operation. \\
\hline
{\em flatten\+\_\+kw\+\_\+ratio} & Frequency scaling of the flattening noise field. \\
\hline
{\em flatten\+\_\+amp} & Amplitude control of the flattening operation. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to a noise field used to displace grid coordinates in X. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to a noise field used to displace grid coordinates in Y. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & The 2D bounding box (\{xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax\}) over which the terrain is generated.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A procedurally generated {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} representing the synthetic basalt-\/like terrain field.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This function relies on Open\+CL-\/based kernels via the {\ttfamily gpu\+:\+:} namespace.
\item The returned field is normalized in amplitude but may require rescaling to match specific physical units.
\item Adjusting {\ttfamily seed}, {\ttfamily warp\+\_\+kw}, and the gain/amplitude values can produce a wide variety of terrain features.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

{\bfseries{Result}}  \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a50db0e092d6e8d147a587b18ee7ea743}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a50db0e092d6e8d147a587b18ee7ea743}

\index{gabor\_wave@{gabor\_wave}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gabor\_wave()}{gabor\_wave()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::gabor\+\_\+wave (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{angle,  }\item[{float}]{angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return an array filled with coherence Gabor noise. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} shape. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Noise wavenumbers \{kx, ky\} for each directions. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed number. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Base orientation angle for the Gabor wavelets (in radians). Defaults to 0. \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio} & Ratio that controls the spread of wave orientations around the base angle. Defaults to 1. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Domain bounding box. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} Fractal noise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://www.shadertoy.com/view/clGyWm}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+shadertoy.\+com/view/cl\+Gy\+Wm}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::gabor\+\_\+wave (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{angle = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a9a67e946fa8616f634c1e5f1cad6045b}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a9a67e946fa8616f634c1e5f1cad6045b}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gabor\_wave\_fbm()}{gabor\_wave\_fbm()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::gabor\+\_\+wave\+\_\+fbm (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \&}]{angle,  }\item[{float}]{angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{weight = {\ttfamily 0.7\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{persistence = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return an array filled with coherence Gabor noise. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} shape. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Noise wavenumbers \{kx, ky\} for each directions. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed number. \\
\hline
{\em angle} & Base orientation angle for the Gabor wavelets (in radians). Defaults to 0. \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio} & Ratio that controls the spread of wave orientations around the base angle. Defaults to 1. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of octaves. \\
\hline
{\em weigth} & Octave weighting. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Octave persistence. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Defines the wavenumber ratio between each octaves. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Reference to the control parameter array (acts as a multiplier for the weight parameter). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x,p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Reference to the input noise arrays. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Domain bounding box. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} Fractal noise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://www.shadertoy.com/view/clGyWm}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+shadertoy.\+com/view/cl\+Gy\+Wm}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a 2D array using the Gavoro\+Noise algorithm, which is a procedural noise technique for terrain generation and other applications. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Dimensions of the output array. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Wave number vector controlling the noise frequency. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Seed value for random number generation. \\
\hline
{\em amplitude} & Amplitude of the noise. \\
\hline
{\em kw\+\_\+multiplier} & Multiplier for wave numbers in the noise function. \\
\hline
{\em slope\+\_\+strength} & Strength of slope-\/based directional erosion in the noise. \\
\hline
{\em branch\+\_\+strength} & Strength of branch-\/like structures in the generated noise. \\
\hline
{\em z\+\_\+cut\+\_\+min} & Minimum cutoff for Z-\/value in the noise. \\
\hline
{\em z\+\_\+cut\+\_\+max} & Maximum cutoff for Z-\/value in the noise. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of octaves for fractal Brownian motion (f\+Bm). \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Amplitude scaling factor between noise octaves. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Frequency scaling factor between noise octaves. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Optional array for control parameters, can modify the Z cutoff dynamically. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional array for X-\/axis noise perturbation. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional array for Y-\/axis noise perturbation. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box for mapping grid coordinates to world space.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D array containing the generated Gavoro\+Noise values.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://www.shadertoy.com/view/MtGcWh}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+shadertoy.\+com/view/\+Mt\+Gc\+Wh}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}
This function leverages an Open\+CL kernel to compute the Gavoro\+Noise values on the GPU, allowing for efficient large-\/scale generation. The kernel applies a combination of fractal Brownian motion (f\+Bm), directional erosion, and other procedural techniques to generate intricate noise patterns.

The optional {\ttfamily p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param}, {\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x}, and {\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} buffers provide additional flexibility for dynamically adjusting noise parameters and perturbations.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mountain\_range\_radial()}{mountain\_range\_radial()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::mountain\+\_\+range\+\_\+radial (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{half\+\_\+width = {\ttfamily 0.2\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{core\+\_\+size\+\_\+ratio = {\ttfamily 1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{center = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{weight = {\ttfamily 0.7\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{persistence = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+angle = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a heightmap representing a radial mountain range. 

This function creates a heightmap that simulates a mountain range emanating radially from a specified center. The mountain range is influenced by various noise parameters and control attributes.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The dimensions of the output heightmap as a 2D vector. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & The wave numbers (frequency components) as a 2D vector. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & The seed for random noise generation. \\
\hline
{\em half\+\_\+width} & The half-\/width of the radial mountain range, controlling its spread. Default is 0.\+2f. \\
\hline
{\em angle\+\_\+spread\+\_\+ratio} & The ratio controlling the angular spread of the mountain range. Default is 0.\+5f. \\
\hline
{\em center} & The center point of the radial mountain range as normalized coordinates within \mbox{[}0, 1\mbox{]}. Default is \{0.\+5f, 0.\+5f\}. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & The number of octaves for fractal noise generation. Default is 8. \\
\hline
{\em weight} & The initial weight for noise contribution. Default is 0.\+7f. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & The amplitude scaling factor for subsequent noise octaves. Default is 0.\+5f. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & The frequency scaling factor for subsequent noise octaves. Default is 2.\+0f. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Optional pointer to an array of control parameters influencing the terrain generation. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to a precomputed noise array for the X-\/axis. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to a precomputed noise array for the Y-\/axis. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+angle} & Optional pointer to an array to output the angle. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & The bounding box of the output heightmap in normalized coordinates \mbox{[}xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax\mbox{]}. Default is \{0.\+0f, 1.\+0f, 0.\+0f, 1.\+0f\}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} The generated heightmap representing the radial mountain range.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ "{}\mbox{\hyperlink{highmap_8hpp}{highmap.hpp}}"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\index{vorolines@{vorolines}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vorolines()}{vorolines()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::vorolines (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{float}]{density,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{exp\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{alpha = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{alpha\+\_\+span = {\ttfamily M\+\_\+PI},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2f}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type}}}]{return\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox\+\_\+points = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a Voronoi-\/based pattern where cells are defined by proximity to random lines. 

This function generates an Open\+CL-\/accelerated Voronoi-\/like pattern based on the distance from each pixel to a set of randomly oriented lines. Each line is defined by a random point and a direction sampled from a uniform distribution around a given angle.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The resolution of the resulting 2D array (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em density} & Number of base points per unit area used to define lines. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Seed for the random number generator used to generate base points and directions. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smoothing} & Kernel smoothing factor; controls how sharp or soft the distance fields are. \\
\hline
{\em exp\+\_\+sigma} & Exponential smoothing parameter applied to the computed distance field. \\
\hline
{\em alpha} & Base angle (in radians) used to orient the generated lines. \\
\hline
{\em alpha\+\_\+span} & Maximum angular deviation from {\ttfamily alpha}; controls line orientation variability. \\
\hline
{\em return\+\_\+type} & Type of Voronoi output to return (e.\+g., F1, F2, edge distance, smoothed field, etc.). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to an input noise field applied to the X coordinates (can be nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to an input noise field applied to the Y coordinates (can be nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box in normalized coordinates (min\+\_\+x, max\+\_\+x, min\+\_\+y, max\+\_\+y) of the final array. \\
\hline
{\em bbox\+\_\+points} & Bounding box within which random base points are sampled.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D array (of type \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}) containing the computed distance field based on line proximity.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Each line is defined from a point (x, y) to a direction offset using angle {\ttfamily theta = alpha + rand \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} alpha\+\_\+span}. 

The Open\+CL kernel "{}vorolines"{} must be defined and compiled beforehand.
\end{DoxyNote}

\{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a Voronoi-\/based pattern using distances to lines defined by random points and angles, with additional fractal Brownian motion (f\+Bm) noise modulation. 

This function extends the standard {\ttfamily vorolines} generation by introducing f\+Bm-\/based warping of the coordinate space, resulting in more organic and fractal-\/like structures. It creates a Voronoi distance field based on proximity to oriented line segments and distorts the result using multi-\/octave procedural noise.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Output resolution of the 2D array (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em density} & Number of base points per unit area used to define lines. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Seed value for the random number generator. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smoothing} & Kernel smoothing coefficient to soften distance values (e.\+g., for blending). \\
\hline
{\em exp\+\_\+sigma} & Sigma value for optional exponential smoothing on the final field. \\
\hline
{\em alpha} & Base orientation angle (in radians) of lines generated from random points. \\
\hline
{\em alpha\+\_\+span} & Maximum angle deviation from {\ttfamily alpha}, determining directional randomness of lines. \\
\hline
{\em return\+\_\+type} & Type of output to return (e.\+g., F1, F2, distance to edge, smoothed version). \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of noise octaves used in the f\+Bm modulation. \\
\hline
{\em weight} & Weight of each octave\textquotesingle{}s contribution to the total noise. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Amplitude decay factor for each successive octave (commonly 0.\+5–0.8). \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Frequency multiplier for each successive octave (commonly 2.\+0). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to an external noise field applied to X coordinates (can be nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to an external noise field applied to Y coordinates (can be nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box for the final image domain (min\+\_\+x, max\+\_\+x, min\+\_\+y, max\+\_\+y). \\
\hline
{\em bbox\+\_\+points} & Bounding box from which the initial set of points are sampled.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} representing the Voronoi-\/f\+Bm field, distorted by noise and influenced by distance to random lines.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This version uses internally computed f\+Bm noise unless external fields ({\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x}, {\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y}) are provided. 

This function requires an Open\+CL kernel named "{}vorolines\+\_\+fbm"{} to be compiled and accessible.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{voronoi()}{voronoi()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::voronoi (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{jitter = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{exp\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2f}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type}}}]{return\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a Voronoi diagram in a 2D array with configurable properties. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The dimensions of the output array as a 2D vector of integers. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & The frequency scale factors for the Voronoi cells, given as a 2D vector of floats. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & A seed value for random number generation, ensuring reproducibility. \\
\hline
{\em jitter} & (Optional) The amount of random variation in the positions of Voronoi cell sites, given as a 2D vector of floats. Defaults to \{0.\+5f, 0.\+5f\}. \\
\hline
{\em return\+\_\+type} & (Optional) The type of value to compute for the Voronoi diagram. Defaults to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} used to control the Voronoi computation. Used here as a multiplier for the jitter. If nullptr, no control is applied. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} providing additional noise in the x-\/direction for cell positions. If nullptr, no x-\/noise is applied. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} providing additional noise in the y-\/direction for cell positions. If nullptr, no y-\/noise is applied. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & (Optional) The bounding box for the Voronoi computation, given as a 4D vector of floats representing \{min\+\_\+x, max\+\_\+x, min\+\_\+y, max\+\_\+y\}. Defaults to \{0.\+f, 1.\+f, 0.\+f, 1.\+f\}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D array representing the generated Voronoi diagram.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{voronoi\_fbm()}{voronoi\_fbm()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::voronoi\+\_\+fbm (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{jitter = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{exp\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2f}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type}}}]{return\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}},  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{weight = {\ttfamily 0.7\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{persistence = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a Voronoi diagram in a 2D array with configurable properties. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The dimensions of the output array as a 2D vector of integers. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & The frequency scale factors for the base Voronoi cells, given as a 2D vector of floats. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & A seed value for random number generation, ensuring reproducibility. \\
\hline
{\em jitter} & (Optional) The amount of random variation in the positions of Voronoi cell sites, given as a 2D vector of floats. Defaults to \{0.\+5f, 0.\+5f\}. \\
\hline
{\em return\+\_\+type} & (Optional) The type of value to compute for the Voronoi diagram. Defaults to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & (Optional) The number of layers (octaves) in the fractal Brownian motion. Defaults to 8. \\
\hline
{\em weight} & (Optional) The initial weight of the base layer in the FBM computation. Defaults to 0.\+7f. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & (Optional) The persistence factor that controls the amplitude reduction between octaves. Defaults to 0.\+5f. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & (Optional) The lacunarity factor that controls the frequency increase between octaves. Defaults to 2.\+f. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} used to control the Voronoi computation. If nullptr, no control is applied. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} providing additional noise in the x-\/direction for cell positions. If nullptr, no x-\/noise is applied. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & (Optional) A pointer to an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} providing additional noise in the y-\/direction for cell positions. If nullptr, no y-\/noise is applied. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & (Optional) The bounding box for the Voronoi computation, given as a 4D vector of floats representing \{min\+\_\+x, max\+\_\+x, min\+\_\+y, max\+\_\+y\}. Defaults to \{0.\+f, 1.\+f, 0.\+f, 1.\+f\}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A 2D array representing the generated Voronoi diagram.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

{\bfseries{Result}}  \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_aaee46739a429168aa45ff1e5d55041ec}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_aaee46739a429168aa45ff1e5d55041ec} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!voronoi\_edge\_distance@{voronoi\_edge\_distance}}
\index{voronoi\_edge\_distance@{voronoi\_edge\_distance}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{voronoi\_edge\_distance()}{voronoi\_edge\_distance()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::voronoi\+\_\+edge\+\_\+distance (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{kw,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{jitter = {\ttfamily \{0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes the Voronoi edge distance. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The shape of the grid as a 2D vector (width, height). \\
\hline
{\em kw} & The weights for the Voronoi kernel as a 2D vector. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & The random seed used for generating Voronoi points. \\
\hline
{\em jitter} & Optional parameter for controlling jitter in Voronoi point placement (default is \{0.\+5f, 0.\+5f\}). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Optional pointer to an \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} specifying control parameters for Voronoi grid jitter (default is nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x,p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Reference to the input noise arrays. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & The bounding box for the Voronoi diagram as \{x\+\_\+min, x\+\_\+max, y\+\_\+min, y\+\_\+max\} (default is \{0.\+f, 1.\+f, 0.\+f, 1.\+f\}).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://www.shadertoy.com/view/llG3zy}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+shadertoy.\+com/view/ll\+G3zy}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.

The resulting \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} has the same dimensions as the input shape. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a29cc1b0843f7447eb19b6cef27772cdd}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_a29cc1b0843f7447eb19b6cef27772cdd} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!voronoise@{voronoise}}
\index{voronoise@{voronoise}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{voronoise()}{voronoise()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::voronoise (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{kw,  }\item[{float}]{u\+\_\+param,  }\item[{float}]{v\+\_\+param,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a 2D Voronoi noise array. 

This function computes a Voronoi noise pattern based on the input parameters and returns it as a 2D array. The noise is calculated in the Open\+CL kernel {\ttfamily noise\+\_\+voronoise}, which uses a combination of hashing and smoothstep functions to generate a weighted Voronoi noise field.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://www.shadertoy.com/view/Xd23Dh}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+shadertoy.\+com/view/\+Xd23\+Dh}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & The dimensions of the 2D output array as a vector (width and height). \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Wave numbers for scaling the noise pattern, represented as a 2D vector. \\
\hline
{\em u\+\_\+param} & A control parameter for the noise, adjusting the contribution of random offsets. \\
\hline
{\em v\+\_\+param} & A control parameter for the noise, affecting the smoothness of the pattern. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Optional pointer to an \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} specifying control parameters for Voronoi grid jitter (default is nullptr). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x,p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Reference to the input noise arrays. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & A seed value for random number generation, ensuring reproducibility.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} object containing the generated 2D Voronoi noise values.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::voronoise\+\_\+fbm (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ float $>$}]{kw,  }\item[{float}]{u\+\_\+param,  }\item[{float}]{v\+\_\+param,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{int}]{octaves = {\ttfamily 8},  }\item[{float}]{weight = {\ttfamily 0.7\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{persistence = {\ttfamily 0.5\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{lacunarity = {\ttfamily 2.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return an array filled with coherence Voronoise. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} shape. \\
\hline
{\em kw} & Noise wavenumbers \{kx, ky\} for each directions. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Random seed number. \\
\hline
{\em octaves} & Number of octaves. \\
\hline
{\em weigth} & Octave weighting. \\
\hline
{\em persistence} & Octave persistence. \\
\hline
{\em lacunarity} & Defines the wavenumber ratio between each octaves. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+ctrl\+\_\+param} & Reference to the control parameter array (acts as a multiplier for the weight parameter). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x,p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Reference to the input noise arrays. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Domain bounding box. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array} Fractal noise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Taken from \href{https://www.shadertoy.com/view/clGyWm}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+shadertoy.\+com/view/cl\+Gy\+Wm}}

Only available if Open\+CL is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

{\bfseries{Result}}  \Hypertarget{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ad25e08146acf2dc7101ec18dbfaa0d2b}\label{namespacehmap_1_1gpu_ad25e08146acf2dc7101ec18dbfaa0d2b} 
\index{hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}!vororand@{vororand}}
\index{vororand@{vororand}!hmap::gpu@{hmap::gpu}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vororand()}{vororand()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} hmap\+::gpu\+::vororand (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec2}{Vec2}}$<$ int $>$}]{shape,  }\item[{float}]{density,  }\item[{float}]{variability,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{array_8hpp_a91ad9478d81a7aaf2593e8d9c3d06a14}{uint}}}]{seed,  }\item[{float}]{k\+\_\+smoothing = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{float}]{exp\+\_\+sigma = {\ttfamily 0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2f}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type}}}]{return\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehmap_a8e3756915e28aa80cec2190043cc8c2fa3e5996ed4314058911435c50bc95e1c2}{Voronoi\+Return\+Type\+::\+F1\+\_\+\+SQUARED}}},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structhmap_1_1Vec4}{Vec4}}$<$ float $>$}]{bbox\+\_\+points = {\ttfamily \{0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~0.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}},~1.\mbox{\hyperlink{distance__transform_8cpp_abcb9259cf91bfd25e92a72cdf18c285e}{f}}\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a 2D Voronoi-\/based scalar field using Open\+CL. 

This function computes a Voronoi diagram or derived metric (such as F1, F2, or edge distances) on a grid of given shape. A set of random points is generated within an extended bounding box, based on the desired density and variability, to reduce edge artifacts. Optionally, per-\/pixel displacement can be applied through noise fields.

The result is stored in an {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} object representing a 2D scalar field.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em shape} & Dimensions of the output array (width x height). \\
\hline
{\em density} & Number of random points per unit area for Voronoi diagram. \\
\hline
{\em variability} & Amount of randomness added to the point generation bounding box. \\
\hline
{\em seed} & Seed for random number generation used in point sampling. \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+smoothing} & Smoothing factor used in soft minimum/maximum Voronoi distance computations. \\
\hline
{\em exp\+\_\+sigma} & Standard deviation used in exponential falloff for edge distance computation. \\
\hline
{\em return\+\_\+type} & Type of Voronoi computation to perform (e.\+g., F1, F2, F2-\/\+F1, edge distance). \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} & Optional pointer to a noise field applied to X coordinates of grid points. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} & Optional pointer to a noise field applied to Y coordinates of grid points. \\
\hline
{\em bbox} & Bounding box of the domain in which the field is computed\+: \{xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax\}. \\
\hline
{\em bbox\+\_\+points} & Bounding box for point generation, usually larger than {\ttfamily bbox} to avoid edge effects.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An {\ttfamily \doxylink{classhmap_1_1Array}{Array}} object containing the computed scalar field.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The kernel {\ttfamily "{}vororand"{}} must be compiled and available in the Open\+CL context.
\item If {\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+x} or {\ttfamily p\+\_\+noise\+\_\+y} are provided, they must match the shape of the output array.
\item The generated point cloud will be larger than {\ttfamily bbox} to reduce border artifacts.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
